In particular,\n903:      * if a transactional send finishes with a {@link ProducerFencedException}, a {@link org.apache.kafka.common.errors.OutOfOrderSequenceException},\n904:      * a {@link org.apache.kafka.common.errors.UnsupportedVersionException}, or an\n905:      * {@link org.apache.kafka.common.errors.AuthorizationException}, then the only option left is to call {@link #close()}.\n906:      * Fatal errors cause the producer to enter a defunct state in which future API calls will continue to raise\n907:      * the same underlying error wrapped in a new {@link KafkaException}.\n908:      * </p>\n909:      * <p>\n910:      * It is a similar picture when idempotence is enabled, but no <code>transactional.id</code> has been configured.\n911:      * In this case, {@link org.apache.kafka.common.errors.UnsupportedVersionException} and\n912:      * {@link org.apache.kafka.common.errors.AuthorizationException} are considered fatal errors. However,\n913:      * {@link ProducerFencedException} does not need to be handled. Additionally, it is possible to continue\n914:      * sending after receiving an {@link org.apache.kafka.common.errors.OutOfOrderSequenceException}, but doing so\n915:      * can result in out of order delivery of pending messages. To ensure proper ordering, you should close the\n916:      * producer and create a new instance.\n917:      * </p>\n918:      * <p>\n919:      * If the message format of the destination topic is not upgraded to 0.11.0.0, idempotent and transactional\n920:      * produce requests will fail with an {@link org.apache.kafka.common.errors.UnsupportedForMessageFormatException}\n921:      * error. If this is encountered during a transaction, it is possible to abort and continue. But note that future\n922:      * sends to the same topic will continue receiving the same exception until the topic is upgraded.\n923:      * </p>\n924:      * <p>\n925:      * Note that callbacks will generally execute in the I/O thread of the producer and so should be reasonably fast or\n926:      * they will delay the sending of messages from other threads. If you want to execute blocking or computationally\n927:      * expensive callbacks it is recommended to use your own {@link java.util.concurrent.Executor} in the callback body\n928:      * to parallelize processing.\n929:      *\n930:      * @param record The record to send\n931:      * @param callback A user-supplied callback to execute when the record has been acknowledged by the server (null\n932:      *        indicates no callback)\n933:      *\n934:      * @throws IllegalStateException if a transactional.id has been configured and no transaction has been started, or\n935:      *                               when send is invoked after producer has been closed.\n936:      * @throws InterruptException If the thread is interrupted while blocked\n937:      * @throws SerializationException If the key or value are not valid objects given the configured serializers\n938:      * @throws KafkaException If a Kafka related error occurs that does not belong to the public API exceptions.\n939:      */\n940:     @Override\n941:     public Future<RecordMetadata> send(ProducerRecord<K, V> record, Callback callback) {\n942:         // intercept the record, which can be potentially modified; this method does not throw exceptions\n943:         ProducerRecord<K, V> interceptedRecord = this.interceptors.onSend(record);\n944:         return doSend(interceptedRecord, callback);\n945:     }\n946: \n947:     // Verify that this producer instance has not been closed. This method throws IllegalStateException if the producer\n948:     // has already been closed.\n949:     private void throwIfProducerClosed() {\n950:         if (sender == null || !sender.isRunning())\n951:             throw new IllegalStateException(\"Cannot perform operation after producer has been closed\");\n952:     }\n953: \n954:     /**\n955:      * Throws an exception if the transaction is in a prepared state.\n956:      * In a two-phase commit (2PC) flow, once a transaction enters the prepared state,\n957:      * only commit, abort, or complete operations are allowed.\n958:      *\n959:      * @throws IllegalStateException if any other operation is attempted in the prepared state.\n960:      */\n961:     private void throwIfInPreparedState() {\n962:         if (transactionManager != null &&\n963:             transactionManager.isTransactional() &&\n964:             transactionManager.isPrepared()\n965:         ) {\n966:             throw new IllegalStateException(\"Cannot perform operation while the transaction is in a prepared state. \" +\n967:                 \"Only commitTransaction(), abortTransaction(), or completeTransaction() are permitted.\");\n968:         }\n969:     }\n970: \n971:     /**\n972:      * Implementation of asynchronously send a record to a topic.\n973:      */\n974:     private Future<RecordMetadata> doSend(ProducerRecord<K, V> record, Callback callback) {\n975:         // Append callback takes care of the following:\n976:         //  - call interceptors and user callback on completion\n977:         //  - remember partition that is calculated in RecordAccumulator.append\n978:         AppendCallbacks appendCallbacks = new AppendCallbacks(callback, this.interceptors, record);\n979: \n980:         try {\n981: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/kafka--0753c489@31d9200189f81283bf60e929ddc38fd68ac034e2/-/blob/clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/producer/KafkaProducer.java%3FL820-980"}}}
